problem #0: MS excel does not get confused by newline characters becasue the text lines are surrounded by quotation marks. In order to remove newline from text field, first go to a new column, then type: =SUBSTITUTE(E2,CHAR(IO), " ") , then format cells , then wrap text in order to check if there is anymore newline, and finally save the file.
